Japanese Troops in North China: Exercise Occupation of Tianjin: Red and White Armies Engaged in Several Fierce Battles: Plainclothes Units Also Participated in Combat: Dense Gunfire, Realistic Situation.

Tianjin Correspondence: The Japanese garrison in North China is holding a major exercise. The first section, a joint exercise of the linked regiments, began on the 26th, simultaneously in Tianjin and Beiping, and ended late on the 28th. The troops rested on the 29th. On the morning of the 30th, the second section of the regiment anti-confrontation exercise began, with Fengtai, Changxindian, and Lugouqiao, where the Beiliu Road, Pinghan Road, Ping Sui Road, and Pingjin Road cross the tracks, as the center of contention. On the morning of the 31st, fierce battles were held again at the Yongding River and Lugouqiao, with engineers building rafts and bridges and forcibly crossing the river, applying modern tactics as a large-scale field battle, which ended that evening. Japanese Commander Tadashi ordered Chief of Staff Hashimoto, Senior Staff Officer Iida, Section Chief Sentada, and other relevant staff officers to go to Tongzhou on the morning of the 2nd. A command headquarters was established in the local special affairs agency to direct the major exercise of the entire Japanese garrison in North China. The puppet Ji Army government, for the sake of driving the workforce, established a Japanese Military Exercise Support Association, which was responsible for handling all matters related to the exercise supply, led by Wang Jizhang, the puppet Tongzhou County Governor. The intentions behind the joint exercise of the Tianjin suburban linked regiment from the 26th to the 28th are extremely profound, which are described in detail below.

The Japanese troops participating in the Tianjin suburban exercise were divided into Red and White teams. According to the hypothetical strategy of the military headquarters' combat section, the Red Army was the main defender, and the White Army was the attacker. At the same time, it was assumed that the Red Army was us and the White Army was the Japanese, with the goal of contending for Tianjin. The units in charge of the attacking army were the Shanhaiguan, Tanggu, and Tangshan guard troops, numbering more than 800 people, linked to more than 700 special branch troops from Lü, Tang, and Qin, for a total of more than 1,500 people. The units in charge of the defending army were the troops stationed in the Tianjin Haiguang Temple and Dongjuzi barracks, numbering about 1,800 people. The remaining chemical warfare, tank, engineer, and communications squads were also separately added to both sides. The exercise began at 6:00 AM on the 26th, assuming that the White Army attacked from the sea and landed at Tanggu, intending to occupy Tianjin. The Red Army received the report and urgently mobilized a large number of troops, rushed to the suburbs of Tianjin to deploy defenses, and the two sides had an unexpected encounter battle near Junliangcheng on the Tangjin section of the Beining Road. The White Army reinforcement troops also arrived from Shanhaiguan, using chemical warfare equipment to cooperate in a fierce attack. The Red Army then changed its strategy, using a large cavalry detour, went out from Lutai in Ninghe County, and cut off the Tang Yu connection between the White Army. As a result, the White Army retreated and gathered between Tang Zhan and Xianshugou to wait for the enemy. That evening, the president of the Tianjin Japan Reservists Association, Tamura, summoned 420 reservists, linked the volunteer corps, the Ji Bei Riding Society, the National Defense Women's Association, and more than a thousand armed expatriates, organized a plainclothes team, assumed that the Red Army was the enemy, and specially disturbed the Tianjin suburbs of Dazhigu and Sunzhuang, etc., for support and defense. The White Army in the Xianshugou area also harassed the Red Army's positions with a small number of troops, resulting in skirmishes and night battles. At 7:00 AM on the 27th, the Red Army dug trenches in the Chentangzhuang, Xianshugou, and Junliangcheng areas for a long-term defense. The White Army then launched a fierce attack with tanks, armored vehicles, and field artillery, causing the Red Army to fall into a bitter battle. The White Army cavalry also detoured from Junliangcheng separately, and the reservists also succeeded in their support and defense activities. At this point, the Red Army felt the pressure of artillery fire and the rear defense was shaken, so it abandoned the Xianshugou position and retreated. On this day of the exercise, traffic within 50 miles of Xianshu was completely cut off. The density of the artillery fire was heard for dozens of miles, and the scene was realistic, almost no different from actual combat. Hashimoto, Chief of Staff of the Japanese Garrison, led staff officers Adachi, Kai, attached officer Suzuki, and Nagamine to inspect in the morning, and gave instructions to the commander of the attacking army, Tangshan's Shinobe, and the commander of the defending army, Huangdao, the commander of the Tianjin Second Regiment. The exercise on the 28th, continued the items of the 26th and 27th from 10:00 AM, as the final decisive battle. The Red Army launched a counterattack towards Xianshugou and Junliangcheng separately, and defended Dazhigu and Dongjuzi to form a triangular position. The Japanese army advanced along the Haihe River and the Beining Road with two wings, and contacted the reservists in Tianjin, breaking the Red Army in Junliangcheng and Dazhi at once. The Red Army then retreated along the Pingjin road to Yangcun and Beicang. After that, they continued to exercise the pursuit battle. The White Army headquarters entered Tianjin, assuming cooperation with the reservists, the National Defense Women's Association, and the Volunteer Corps to search for the remaining enemies and occupy Tianjin. On the one hand, they pursued along the enemy's retreat route. After the Red Army was defeated, they collected troops in Yangcun and Beicang for the final resistance. After 9:00 PM, until 3:00 AM on the 29th, night battles took place in Yangcun and Beicang, with field artillery firing light-emitting bombs and incendiary bombs to exhaust the effectiveness of the new weapons. On the 29th, the troops from Jin, Tang, Yu, and Tang were transported to the Houtai area of Beiping. At 0:50 AM, 700 infantry and artillerymen, 50 horses, and 6 field guns were loaded on a special train and opened to Anding. At 1:30 AM, there were 70 infantrymen and 140 horses, which also opened to Anding. At 3:00 AM, 160 artillerymen, 8 heavy guns, and 5 trucks were loaded on a special train and opened to Anding. At 3:40 AM, 6 field guns, 70 artillerymen, and 16 armored vehicles were loaded on a special train and opened to Anding. At 7:00 AM, 120 Tanggu cavalrymen, 800 Tianjin infantrymen, and 4 field guns were taken by the Ping Shen second train to Anding, and the command headquarters of the Second Regiment was placed in Anding as the rear defense. From the morning of the 30th, they advanced to Fengtai and fought against the First Regiment of Beiping. The command headquarters of the brigade commander Kawabe was established at Fengtai Railway Station on the 29th. (29th)

The Fiftieth Birthday of Chairman Chiang: Celebrations in Full Swing in the City; Banquet and Merriment Held; Delegation Presenting Aircraft Departed for the Capital Last Night; Muslims Offer Birthday Blessings and Prayers for World Peace; Citizens' Federation Petitions the Central Government for Amnesty

Today is Chairman Chiang's fiftieth birthday. At 9:00 AM, a ceremony for presenting aircraft in honor of Chairman Chiang's birthday will be held in the capital. Representatives from Shanghai presenting ten aircraft, including Wu Tiecheng, departed for the capital last night. The Shanghai citizens' celebration and gathering for Chairman Chiang's fiftieth birthday took place at 2:00 PM in the Huangjia Garden in Caohejing. The Party members' celebration banquet for Chairman Chiang's fiftieth birthday was held at 6:30 PM at the Atlantic Western Restaurant on Fuzhou Road. The Municipal Government gathered its affiliated personnel at 12:00 PM in the auditorium of the city center for a luncheon to extend congratulations. The General Labor Union, the Ningbo Native Association, the Seafarers' Organizations, and personnel from both railways also held separate celebrations. Envoys from various countries in Shanghai sent congratulatory telegrams. Muslims also jointly prayed for world peace in the afternoon at the mosque to celebrate Chairman Chiang's birthday. Details are recorded as follows:

Mayor Wu and Others Departed for the Capital Last Night

Today marks Chairman Chiang's fiftieth birthday. The aircraft presentation ceremony is scheduled for 9:00 AM at the Ming Palace Airport in Nanjing. The ten aircraft presented by Shanghai, named Shanghai Municipal Government, Shanghai Party Headquarters, Shanghai Police, Shanghai Commerce, Ningbo, Tourism, Grain, Training Students, and Xiang Chengyi, flew from Hangzhou to the capital yesterday for the presentation. Additionally, the 50,000 yuan donated by Catholics to purchase two ambulance aircraft was entrusted by the City Aircraft Purchase Birthday Celebration Committee to the Chairman Chiang Birthday Aircraft Presentation Commemoration Committee for handling. It is reported that the representatives from various agencies and organizations presenting the aircraft and birthday wishes, including Mayor Wu Tiecheng, as well as Tong Xingbai, Wang Xiaolai, Chuan Xiaoan, Sun Qiuping, Gu Xinyi, Zhu Xilian, Zhu Zigao, Li Dachao, Yu Bin, Lu Bohong, Lu Yigeng, and others, departed for the capital last night by overnight train to participate.

Citywide Party Members Enthusiastically Celebrate

Yesterday, the City Party Headquarters erected a large archway with five emblems in front of its main gate to show celebration. It has been decided that a celebratory banquet will be held tonight at 6:30 PM at the Atlantic Western Restaurant on Simalu. The hall has already been decorated. The area around the main gate of the restaurant on Simalu has been adorned with lanterns and colorful decorations, as well as electric lights. In the center of the hall hangs the Party and National flag and a portrait of Vice-Chairman Chiang, with a large neon寿 (longevity) character in the middle. The entire hall is filled with Party and National flags, creating a very enthusiastic scene.

Envoys from Various Countries in Shanghai Send Congratulatory Telegrams

Today is Chairman Chiang's fiftieth birthday. Diplomatic representatives from various countries stationed in China are celebrating together. It is known that the Italian Ambassador to Shanghai, Luo Yaguonuo, the Polish Minister, Weidengtao, the Czech Minister, Feizheer, the Cuban Minister, Bianda, the Belgian Chargé d'affaires, Tan Er, the Norwegian Chargé d'affaires, Jierde, the Swedish Chargé d'affaires, Beifeilis, the Swiss Chargé d'affaires, Laodi, and the Danish Chargé d'affaires, Xier, have successively sent telegrams to our Foreign Ministry in the past two days, which were then forwarded to Chairman Chiang for congratulations.

Ningbo Native Association Gathering for Merriment

The Ningbo Native Association is celebrating Chiang's birthday today. The association's main gate is decorated with a colorful archway made of pine and cypress, symbolizing evergreen longevity. The auditorium is located where major newspapers have reported. The station frequency is 900 kilocycles, and the call sign is XGOI.

Madam Chiang Soong Meiling Flew to Luoyang Yesterday Morning

Madam Chiang Soong Meiling, the wife of Chairman Chiang, stayed in Shanghai for rest and to handle personal affairs after accompanying Chairman Chiang from Hangzhou to Shanghai. Because today is the Chairman's birthday, she took a specially prepared Junkers aircraft from Hongqiao Airport at 8:00 AM yesterday morning, departing Shanghai and flying to Luoyang to meet Chairman Chiang for a reunion and celebration. Song Ziliang, the Director of the Guangdong Finance Department, Cai Jingjun, the Director of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, Wang Zhinan from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, the sons and daughters of Minister Kong, and Wei Daoming, Zheng Yuxiu, and others came to see her off. The airport was temporarily under guard.

Performing Arts Association Celebrates with Broadcasting

The Shanghai Performing Arts Association, including various troupes affiliated with the Shanghai Opera, Suzhou Ballad, One-Man Show, Drama, Runyu Society, Yongyu Society, Improved Ningbo Opera, Huaiyang Storytelling, and Story Broadcasting, as well as over ten thousand members, together with the Shanghai Social Education Society, held a broadcasting celebration at the New Sound Radio Station (frequency 1380) today. It started from 1:00 PM this afternoon and lasted until 3:00 AM the next morning. In addition to sending congratulatory telegrams, they also reported to the Party and government organs and the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau for record.

The Deployment of the Japanese Army's Large-Scale Exercise in North China: An Unprecedented Event Since the Boxer Rebellion

This time, the Japanese army conducted a large-scale exercise in the vicinity of Beiping (now Beijing), Hebei Province, with over 7,000 participants. For about ten days, everything centered around Beiping. The grandeur of the military presence, the precision of the deployment, and even the participation of chemical warfare units represented an unprecedented move by foreign troops in China since the Boxer Rebellion. The foreign armies' ability to station troops in Tianjin and Beiping stemmed from the anti-foreign sentiment of the Boxer Rebellion and was stipulated in the Boxer Protocol of 1901. However, the spirit of the agreement was merely to maintain transportation between Tianjin and Beiping. Therefore, although various countries had troops stationed there, the numbers were very limited. Leisurely drills were mostly confined to the Legation Quarter and its surrounding open spaces (the open space around the Legation Quarter was not allowed to have buildings constructed, which was also recognized at the time, to meet the security needs of the legation area). During their spare time they went to the Babaoshan ball field, and annual exercises were mostly conducted near the Shanhai Pass. There was never a case of troops openly displaying their armor near Beiping. In recent years, Japan has expanded its military presence, initially using the Boxer Protocol as an excuse, and then moving forward without restraint, continuously increasing its troop numbers. Furthermore, it has taken another step by stationing troops in Fengtai and conducting exercises in the suburbs of Beiping. Although we have records of this exercise, they are often vague and lack detail, insufficient for the general public's understanding of military affairs. Here, we present the basic operational table and a simplified map of the exercise for the readers to study, hoping they can gain some insight into the situation.

Basic Table of Operations for the Japanese Garrison Army's Autumn Exercise

Exercise Overview

26th: 8:00 AM to 2:00 PM, areas west of Beiping and north of Fengtai.

27th: Departing separately from Beiping and Tongzhou, gathering in areas near Dongzhen before 2:00 PM. Camping that night centered around Dongzhen and its vicinity.

28th: A portion in Tongzhou, the main force in Shandongchangzhen (6:00 AM to 1:00 PM). Part of the artillery camped near Juetaikou.

29th: From the morning of the 29th to the morning of the 30th, camped in Hou'anding and Qian'anding.

30th: From morning until night of the same day, in the area between the northwest of Majuqiao and Dahongmen.

31st: Rest at Majuqiao in the morning.

From the evening of the 1st to the morning of the 3rd: Part of the force camped in Fengtai.

22nd to 4th: Departing from Tongzhou, exercising from the south and southwest of Huaiping until the morning of the 4th. Exercise west of Beiping until 10:00 AM on the 4th. Conducted a parade.

Suzhou: Reconstructing the Wannian Bridge with Labor and Funding

Due to merchant requests, Wuxian Construction has begun reconstruction of the Wannian Bridge outside Xumen, which is the most heavily traveled bridge. The bridge will be lowered by five feet and replaced with a wooden surface. The estimated cost is 9,500 yuan, with work scheduled to begin on November 1st. However, the contractor had already dismantled the bridge surface before building a pontoon bridge, obstructing traffic. Therefore, the business community inside and outside Xumen expressed opposition, demanding that the construction bureau build a pontoon bridge first. They also suggested changing the bridge surface to reinforced concrete for a permanent solution, with the necessary funds raised by the business community. The construction bureau considered this matter to be difficult to change after reporting it to the construction department. Building a pontoon bridge would be costly due to the wide river surface. Therefore, a changed method was to set up four ferries to transport passengers and facilitate transportation. This has been resolved and construction will begin immediately, with completion expected in two months.

Kunshan: Young Woman Jumps from Train in Suicide Attempt

At 6:15 PM on the 28th, a train on the Jinxi Line, departing from Shanghai, was passing through Anting Station in the county's third district when suddenly a young woman jumped from the window in a suicide attempt. Fortunately, a passenger noticed and quickly alerted the driver to apply the brakes. The attendants then helped the woman up, seeing that her face was badly scraped and bleeding profusely, and she had also suffered internal injuries. She was later put back on the train to Suzhou for medical treatment. It is reported that the woman's name is Zai Qian, 21 years old, from Suzhou. Because her parents prevented her from pursuing further studies, she developed suicidal thoughts.

Changzhou: Widening Streets in Busy City Center

Within Wuyi County, Dajie (Main Street), Fuzhijie (Prefecture Direct Street), Juqianjie (Bureau Front Street), and Xianhengjie (County Horizontal Street) are the busiest. Recently, the county government drafted a plan to widen the streets, which was discussed and approved at the administrative meeting on the 29th. The following is an excerpt of the plan: (1) Road width: Dajie, Fuzhijie, Beihoujie (North Back Street), Juqianjie, Xianhengjie - 8 meters for the roadway, 2 meters for the sidewalk on each side. (2) Expenses: The construction expenses will be borne 40% by the government and 60% by the residents on both sides, calculated based on the average frontage. If not self-produced, then shared jointly according to the Sixth Code. (3) Engineering plan: The road surface will be paved with cobblestones, and the sidewalks will be paved with yellow bricks or cement. (4) Drains: The main drain will be improved based on the original main drain, and side drains will be added every 25 meters. (5) Bridges: The county will allocate funds from the construction expenses to rebuild them. (6) Free building permits will be allowed when demolishing houses, and demolition costs will be handled in accordance with the average profit and loss rules for urban road construction land in Jiangsu Province. It is also heard that the county government will submit the approved plan to the provincial department for review and approval before announcing the widening and starting construction.

Wuxi: Celebrating Chiang Kai-shek's Birthday with Jubilation

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the Wuxi County Government convened a preparatory meeting for all sectors of Wuxi to celebrate Chiang Kai-shek's birthday. The chairman was Long Tiyao, and the following resolutions were made: (1) A celebration will be held at the Zhongnan Theater at 9:00 AM on October 31st. (2) The Public Security Bureau is responsible for arranging the venue and setting up a longevity hall. (3) The title of the celebration ceremony will be "Celebrating Chairman Chiang's Birthday." (4) Slogans will be drafted by the Political Training Office of the 88th Division and the County Party Headquarters. (5) The Commissioner's Office, County Party Headquarters, County Government, 88th Division, and Political Training Office will form the presidium of the conference. (6) The people of the county will warmly celebrate, with the County Propaganda Department preparing slogans and leaflets to promote Chiang Kai-shek's achievements. The County Government will order all district offices to use the baojia system to inform all merchants and residents in the county to hang flags and lanterns to celebrate, and factories will sound sirens during the meeting to express their respect. (7) Zhang Da was designated as the general commander of the parade. (8) The number of participants in the conference will be 20 from each school, full participation from each government agency, and 2 to 5 from each public organization. (9) The expenses will be borne half by the County Government and half by the various bureaus and Party Headquarters. At the same time, Commissioner Zang, along with the county heads of eight counties, telegraphed the Nanjing Executive Yuan to offer congratulations.

Large Quantities of Grain Leaving the Country

This county is a center for the collection of rice and grain, and a large number of rice and grain from various places are transported to Wuxi for sale. Therefore, every time new grain enters the market, rice shops try their best to purchase goods, and warehouses are filled to capacity, causing market prices to fall. Although this year's new harvest is more abundant than in previous years, the sources from various ports are extremely scarce, and the consumption is quite good, resulting in a firm market in this city. In recent days, batches of rice and paddy have been loaded and transported out of the country, reportedly heading to Chang'an, Luoyang, Tongshan, and other places. Within these five days, 800 tons have been shipped out every day, all using train carriages. It is evident that the amount shipped out this month is quite astonishing. In addition, the market price of flour has also increased due to brisk sales. The reason for the brisk sales is attributed to the strong purchasing power of Shaanxi, Luoyang, Weinan, Tongshan, and other places. The amount of flour shipped out yesterday was over 10,000 bags, totaling five train cars. It is said that the amount within these three days is also astonishing. Upon learning of this, the County Party Headquarters immediately dispatched personnel to the train station and warehouses to investigate and take measures to prevent the loading and transportation in order to maintain the people's food supply.

Changshu: The Second Departure of the Malaria Eradication Team

In the fifth and sixth districts of the eastern township of this county, malignant malaria is prevalent this autumn, with successive deaths. The situation is no less severe than the cholera epidemic in the summer. For the sake of providing relief to the poor and sick, the Red Cross branch has specially joined forces with various physicians from the Physicians' Association to go to the countryside to eradicate malaria. The first team left on the 25th, and the second team departed on the 29th. It included physicians such as Wang Siyi, Zhou Xu, Wang Enguang, Yu Jishi, Gu Mansun, and many staff members of the association, who went to Zhitang and Zhangshi and returned to the city on the 30th. In just one day, the number of people seeking treatment reached 274, of whom 44 were injected with malaria treatment drugs. The situation was very crowded. It is heard that the third departure of the team is scheduled for November 3rd.

Yangzhou: Cracking a Case of Instigating Robbery of One's Father

Magistrate Ma Zhenbang of Jiangdu County, due to repeated banditry in the seventh district, ordered the security police captain to rush to investigate. It is now known that the captain led a team of 40 men to the district and apprehended Shen Shirong, a bandit who robbed Wang Guisong, a local villager, of over ten yuan in legal tender and shot Wang Guisong in the waist and head, and also injured Wang's wife, Chen. Shen confessed to being instigated by Wang Chunlin. Wang Chunlin, as well as other suspects in the case, Jiang Chengding, Gu Jiayu, and Wu Zhaoqing, were subsequently apprehended. Wang Chunlin confessed to the instigation. All of the arrested have been transferred to the county government and are awaiting legal proceedings. It is reported that three other bandits are still at large and are being investigated. The victim was afraid of retaliation from the bandits and did not dare to report the case.

Section Chief Accused of Dereliction of Duty

Yao Haicong, Section Chief of the Second Section of the Jiangdu Public Security Bureau, was accused by Liu Shengya, a first-level police officer from the First Precinct, of crimes such as dereliction of duty, assault, illegal detention, and abuse of power. On the afternoon of the 19th, the Public Security Bureau sent a document and dispatched bailiff Guan Jiazhen and police officers Yang Hui and Wang Xinhua to escort the Section Chief to the Jiangdu District Prosecutor's Office. The prosecutor, Xia Weishang, opened the court, summoned the plaintiff's witness, Xu Zhongyuan, to the court for questioning, and ordered Yao to provide two reputable shopkeepers as guarantors and a cash guarantee of 200 yuan. It is heard that because it was difficult to find a guarantor, it was changed to Inspector Meng Shiyu acting as guarantor, and the guarantee was reduced to 150 yuan. As for the details of the case, due to a misunderstanding in which the First Telephone Precinct ordered ten pieces of clothing to be sent to the bureau, Police Officer Liu was beaten eighty times on the palms of his hands, followed by several blows with a stick, and was detained for ten days.

Pinghu: The Closing of the Zhejiang Provincial Private Electricity Industry Association Meeting

Since its establishment, the Zhejiang Provincial Branch of the National Private Electricity Industry Association has held annual meetings in Jiaxing, Wuxing, Ningbo, Shaoxing, Wenzhou, and Xiashi. The eighth annual meeting was held at the Minghua Power Plant in Pinghu. It opened the day before yesterday (26th), with over 300 representatives from the Construction Committee, including Wu Yulin, representative of the Ministry of Communications, Zhu Chongguang, representative of the Construction Department, Lao Naixin, and representatives, members, and guests from all sectors of the Party, government, and military. Yang Yunong, Shen Sifang, Ye Yangwu, Wen Hanpo, and Han Yimin were elected to the presidium, with Shen Sifang presiding and delivering the opening address. He briefly stated that the association was established in the same year as the National Association and has been running for eight years. During these eight years, under the supervision and maintenance of the central and local competent authorities, and with the efforts of the association's colleagues, the electrical industry in Zhejiang Province has made considerable progress. Regrettably, although the central government has various good laws and regulations, such as supervision regulations, rules for dealing with electricity theft, and rules for preventing military police organs and troops from forcibly using electricity, the trend of electricity theft in various places has not subsided slightly. Military police agencies forcibly using electricity and refusing to pay are also frequently heard of. The harsh taxes and miscellaneous fees have not been completely abolished. How to ensure that central laws and regulations are effectively implemented in the future depends on the supervision of the competent authorities and the efforts of the association's colleagues. On the one hand, the industry itself should also step up its work, revitalize its business, reduce costs, and ensure continuous supply, so that users can enjoy affordable benefits. The electrical industry is the lifeline of the country and the foundation of economic construction. In this extraordinary period, it bears a heavier responsibility. Before the fall of the Northeast, the electrical industry was controlled by foreigners. Recently, they have turned their attention to North China. If our private electrical industry cannot revitalize itself, the government does not protect it, and users do not understand it, it will inevitably gradually fail, and foreigners will seize the opportunity to step in and replace it. The degree of danger is really unthinkable. Conversely, China's electrical industry currently has more than 440 companies, with a capital of over 11 million, and hundreds of thousands of employees. If our government can use its talent and resources for the benefit of the country and train them, it can become the greatest force in national defense. The various representatives then delivered speeches, and members and guests gave speeches, which will not be recorded in length. The general meeting of members continued for two days on the 27th and 28th, and closed on the 29th. This time, Shanghai national electrical appliance manufacturers such as Zhonghua, Huade, Huasheng, and Yapuer, all attended the meeting and displayed their products at the venue. Employees of the Shaoxing Daming Company also borrowed the Xinmin Theater to perform for two days to add to the festivities.

Jiaxing: Bureau Official Embezzles and Flees

Chen Wenhui, an official of the Fengqiao Public Security Bureau in Jiaxing, released a suspect, Shi Huchen, after accepting a bribe of 40 yuan, which was paid through Cao Shuping, a clerk from Hanbei Township. Dai Wenhao, the deputy chief of Hanzhong Township, personally requested Wang Mingyi, the director of the Fengqiao Public Security Bureau, to investigate. Wang Xianqiang, the supervisory commissioner, instructed supervisory officers Zhuo Shaosheng and Huang Bingquan to conduct a secret investigation on the spot. The case was verified, and it was also discovered that Chen had privately confiscated fines without issuing receipts in many cases. However, bureau official Chen Wenhui had already fled after committing the crime. Later, it was verified that Shi Huchen and Cao Shuping were indeed involved. Liu Hu presented the report to Commissioner Wang for review and action.

Gu Xingyi Went to Nanjing Last Night to Petition: Zhejiang Releases Rice after Guaranteeing Transport

The Shanghai market was not affected in the short term.

Establish measures for the domestic circulation of rice and wheat.

Gu Xingyi, chairman of the Cereal Association, went to Nanjing last night to petition the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the Executive Yuan to revoke the ban issued by the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The Shanghai Municipal Government has approved the measures for the domestic circulation of rice and wheat. Details are as follows:

Social Affairs Bureau Cables Request for Release

After the Cereal Association dispatched Gu Xingyi and two others to petition the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau the day before yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday telegraphed Xu Qingfu, Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Zhejiang Province, to instruct the county heads of Jiaxing and Pinghu to quickly release the rice ships bound for Shanghai in order to adjust the Shanghai food supply. The Municipal Government yesterday separately telegraphed Chen Guofu and Huang Shaoxiong, the chairmen of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, requesting them to withdraw the order banning rice from leaving the provinces in order to adjust the domestic food supply.

Mr. Gu Takes Advantage of Trip to Nanjing to Petition

Gu Qingyi, Chairman of the Cereal Association, took advantage of his trip to Nanjing as a representative of the grain industry to present an aircraft as a birthday gift, and specially submitted a petition to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the Executive Yuan. In addition to stating the opinion that rice and wheat should be allowed to circulate domestically and banned from export, he also requested the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to revoke the ban and release the detained rice ships. Mr. Gu took the Shanghai-Nanjing express train to Nanjing last night, planning to attend the aircraft presentation ceremony this morning, petition the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the Executive Yuan in the afternoon, and return to Shanghai that night.

Detained Rice Released after Guarantee

A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency learned from the grain industry yesterday that the rice ships bound for Shanghai that were detained in Pinghu and Jiaxing, Zhejiang Province, had been released by the county governments after the local grain industry groups requested it and the rice merchants provided a guarantee. Fortunately, the time of detention and release was very short, so the Shanghai food supply was not affected. As for the Shanghai rice price, it is slightly lower than before. The number one Jiangsu rice is 11 yuan per picul (dan) in national currency, and wheat from Yuansi is about 6.5 yuan, and the recent period is 6 yuan.

Municipal Government Approves Circulation Measures

The four provisional measures for the circulation of rice and wheat within this city proposed by the Cereal Association, after the opinion of Yan Wenkai, director of the Food Division of the Fourth Section of the Social Affairs Bureau, were approved by the bureau director and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval on the 27th. It is heard that the Municipal Government has approved it and ordered the Social Affairs Bureau to handle it in accordance with the measures. The above measures will be implemented on the day they are announced by the Social Affairs Bureau.

Silver and Money Industries Asked President Guo Yesterday to Exempt Cotton Warehouse Receipts from Detention. The Enforcement Officer Immediately Handled the Change. The Exchange Settlement Was Not Affected Yesterday.

The Hua Shang Yarn and Cloth Exchange was ordered by the First Special District Court to detain cotton warehouse receipts. The silver and money industries jointly requested that they be exempted from detention. After the court approved the change, settlement continued as usual yesterday. Details are as follows:

Silver and Money Industries Request Exemption from Detention

The silver and money industries associations decided at a joint meeting to request that the First Special District Court be instructed to exempt the Hua Shang Yarn and Cloth Exchange from detaining cotton warehouse receipts. President Guo agreed that if it was difficult to detain the warehouse receipts, he would decide to handle the change and immediately instructed the enforcement officer to comply.

Settlement Handled as Usual Yesterday

Yesterday was the day for the settlement of yarn and cotton at the Hua Shang Yarn and Cloth Exchange. After the First Special District Court approved the change, settlement continued as usual yesterday without being affected. All Industries are Well Prepared: Steady Passage of the October Credit Period. Shanghai and Ningbo Banks Have Finalized Credit Loans One After Another. The Silver and Money Industries are Busy with Collections and Transfers, and the Exchange Volume Has Increased Sharply.

Today is the October credit long-term loan period for Shanghai industry and commerce. After the various Qianzhuang (traditional Chinese banks) made accommodations, the loan renewal procedures have been completed separately by the borrowers. All industries have passed through the period without any worries. Details are as follows:

Long-Term Credit Finalized One After Another

The member Qianzhuang of the Shanghai Qianzhuang Association, such as the Fuyuanshun Qianzhuang and 47 others, in order to thoroughly support industry and commerce, decided to accommodate the credit long-term loans that are due in October for domestic goods factories, merchants, and companies. The borrowers separately processed the renewal procedures with the Qianzhuang. As of last night, most of them had been processed and were scheduled to be completed by 5:00 PM today. However, the number of recalls and new loans was limited. However, the Ningbo Qianzhuang, who provided credit long-term loans in Shanghai, have also sent personnel to Shanghai to negotiate with the borrowers. The total amount is more than 20 million yuan, with the recall accounting for 40%.

All Industries Pass Through the October Period Without Worries

Since the implementation of the new monetary system policy, all industries have gradually become active. At the same time, all Qianzhuang have accommodated the credit loans that are due, and all industries have passed through the October period without any worries. The foreign exchange market for Qianzhuang is very different from previous years. For example, yesterday the foreign exchange for both the morning and afternoon markets was 8 points, while today last year it was at its highest point of 7 jiao (1 jiao = 1/10 yuan). However, the silver and money industries are busy with collections and transfers due to the October relationship. For example, yesterday the total exchange volume of the bank clearing house was 77,357,064.13 yuan, of which 4,650,920.97 yuan was collected on behalf of the Qianzhuang.

Three Notices from the Lower Bureau

The Public Concession’s Works Department issued three notices regarding the cancellation of one-way traffic on Hankou Road and the regulations for rickshaw fares and rickshaw license fees. The notices are transcribed below:

One-Way Traffic

Notice No. 4756 of the Bureau states: Notice is hereby given that Traffic Rule 46E regarding one-way traffic on Hankou Road, as set forth in Bureau Notice No. 4715 of June 4 of this year, will be canceled from November 1 of this year.

Rickshaw Fares

License Fees

Real Estate Association Submits to the Municipal Government for Assistance in Enforcing Liens

Tenants Evading Rent Damage Landlords - Requesting Police Bureau Attention - The Shanghai Real Estate Industry Association held a special meeting to discuss the issue of landlords' liens on tenants who owe rent and submitted a request to the Municipal Government, requesting the government to order its subordinates to assist in enforcing such rights. The original request stated: Submitted for the matter of tenants evading rent, causing landlords to suffer damage. We earnestly request that you instruct the Public Security Bureau to instruct its branches to pay attention to the legal right of lien and provide assistance in maintaining it. Recently in Shanghai, due to the poor economic situation, many tenants accumulate large amounts of rent arrears. Instead of settling them, they secretly move away with their families. In the short time available, the landlords cannot file a lawsuit in accordance with the law. If they report to the police station and request them to stop the tenant, the police often use the excuse that the matter concerns civil affairs, and even discourage the landlord from exercising the right to retain the tenant's belongings, thus facilitating the tenant's escape. As a result, the landlords suffer losses and have no way to appeal. However, Article 445 of the current Civil Code of China states that the lessor of real estate has a lien on the lessee's belongings placed on the real estate for the debts arising from the lease contract. Article 447 states that if the tenant has the right to object, he may, without petitioning the court, immediately prevent the lessee from taking away the goods subject to the lien. If the lessee leaves the leased real estate, he may also possess the goods. According to the above articles, the landlord naturally has the right to exercise his lien on tenants who secretly move away due to rent arrears. If disputes arise as a result, they must be reported to the police station for assistance in handling the matter and maintaining order. The association has repeatedly received reports from its members about the difficulties encountered, and we earnestly request that you forward them to the government for review and approval, and instruct the Public Security Bureau to instruct its branches to pay special attention to the provisions of Articles 445 and 447 of the Civil Code. In the future, when tenants secretly move away due to rent arrears and the landlord exercises his right of lien in accordance with the law, they should be given full assistance to protect their rights and avoid losses. We await your urgent orders with utmost respect. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government. We also understand that the association has separately sent letters to the French Concession Municipal Council and the Public Concession Works Department, ordering the police stations to assist (text omitted).

Shanghai Municipal Council Health Department to Hire More Chinese Doctors

The SMC Health Department determined that since school medical affairs are increasingly busy, and since the new Chinese Children's School was established on Montauban Road, it is expected that 1,000 Chinese children will enroll next year, therefore the department is unable to cope with the pressure. At the beginning of the year, the Department submitted a request to the Board of Directors, seeking approval to hire one Chinese deputy medical director (including an attendant and a second-class clerk). This matter was approved in principle by the Board of Directors on February 5 of this year, but due to financial constraints, the appointment has not been implemented. Recently, the Director of the Health Department stated that the need is urgent. If the appointment is not implemented, four of the six trachoma treatment centers for schoolchildren currently being operated will have to be closed. There are barely enough personnel to meet the current needs. However, Chinese schoolchildren who suffer from trachoma account for nearly 50%, and blindness among Chinese people is mostly caused by trachoma. Therefore, there is absolutely no reason to stop the treatment of trachoma. After discussion by the Health and Finance Committees, it was agreed that although the financial situation is more difficult than at the beginning of the year, the health of children and the hygiene of citizens are at stake and cannot be stopped. Therefore, the Board of Directors was requested to approve the request so that it could proceed as soon as possible. The Department is expected to make the appointment on January 1 of next year. The total cost is estimated not to exceed 7,200 yuan per year.

Inside Story of the Assassination Case on Jiaozhou Road: The Deceased, Kang Wenjin, Was a Notorious Bandit, Killed Due to a Dispute over Loot and Adultery; The Court Interrogated the Perpetrators Yesterday

At approximately 9:50 PM on the 11th of this month, an assassination occurred at the entrance of Lane 273, Jiaozhou Road, Yanping Road, West Shanghai. A man was found with as many as fifteen or sixteen bullet wounds. When discovered by Chinese constable No. 1920, the man was already dead, and the perpetrators had fled. Therefore, it was difficult to determine the identity of the deceased. Later, the investigators from the Putuo Road Police Station searched the deceased's pockets and found several pieces of paper and train tickets. Through investigation, they learned that the deceased was named Kang Wenjin, residing at No. 940 Dongmali, Binlang Road. However,

How He Was Killed

remained unclear. Last Thursday, Chief Chinese Detective You A'gen, Detectives Li Shugui, Weng Hongxun, and Detective Chen Shanji of the Lao Zha Police Station arrested three Anhui natives, Chen Ruiting, Wu Yuyuan, and Zhang Jinchun, in Dingxiang Lane, Avenue des Soeurs, in the French Concession. A Mauser pistol and ten bullets were found on Zhang, along with a handgun and eleven bullets, and they were handed over to the First Special District Court for detention. After turning over the suspects, the police

Turned Over Two Guns

to the firearms experts for inspection. It was found that the two guns were related to the Lafei Theater robbery on April 19 and the Kang Wenjin assassination case. The detectives then launched an investigation. The results showed that Kang Wenjin, an Anhui native, was a notorious bandit from Zhenjiang. Gu Zhenrong, Niu Min, Zhao Guangzhong, and others were Kang's accomplices. Gu was a Muslim, and his aunt was also married to a Muslim. However, she had an affair with Kang, causing Gu to

Harbor Great Hatred for Kang

but he did not reveal it, so Kang and others remained on good terms. Recently, Kang, Fu, Yang, and Zhao came to Shanghai from Zhenjiang. Kang resided at the home of his fellow villager, Cai Ruhai, at No. 940 Dongmali. On October 10, Zhao Guangzhong invited Chen Ruiting, Wu Jinyuan, and Zhang Chun'an to rob Ma Liangxi's home at an address without a number on Hart Road at 8:30 PM, obtaining 45 yuan in property. This was discovered by Kang, who then wanted to

Share the Loot with Zhao

causing Zhao to also bear a grudge against Kang. Gu Zhenrong also planned to kill Kang to avenge the adultery with his aunt. Therefore, Gu and Zhao agreed with Yang Min, Cai Ruhai, Chen Ruiting, Wu Jinyuan, and Zhang Jinchun that when Kang went to Yanping Road to watch a small Anhui opera on the 11th, Gu and the other seven would falsely claim to Kang that they wanted to rob a certain place and asked Kang to

Go with Them

Kang, unaware of their plan, went along with them. At the time, Gu, Yang, and Zhao

Were Walking in Front

While Chen, Cai, Wu, and Zhang were following behind. When they reached the entrance of Lane 273 on Yanping Road, Gu and the others pulled out their guns and shot at Kang. Because Kang tried to escape, Gu and the others fired wildly, causing Kang to suffer numerous injuries and die on the spot. Gu and the others then scattered and fled. Chen Ruiting also led the detectives to the scene of the crime to demonstrate the situation at the time. Yesterday was the date for the continuation of the trial. Judge Qian Hongye of the First Special Court took his seat in the Criminal Court and interrogated the suspects. Attorney Li Zhishan of the Police Station

Clarified the Previous Events

and filed charges of murder and joint robbery in accordance with Article 271, Paragraph 1, Article 328, and Article 321, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. Ma Liangxi then turned himself in, proving that Wu Jinyuan held the gun during the robbery at the scene. Then, the Western detectives proved the inspection of the gun. Upon questioning Chen Ruiting and Gu Jinchun admitted to participating in the robbery of the Ma family and the murder of Kang Wenjin. Wu Jinyuan was also at the scene, but claimed that he and the others were behind when Kang was killed and did not fire a gun. Wu Jinyuan flatly denied the charges. Judge Qian reviewed the confessions and adjourned the case for further questioning in a week.

Meihua Bank Case: British Director Appears in Court, Submits List of Meihua Shareholders, Says Bao Ziwen and Others Are Directors, But Bao and Others Deny Any Connection

The British-owned Meihua Bank suddenly collapsed before it had been in business for a month. After the Chinese Chairman of the Board, Gu Yubo, fled, the British directors Yelu, Menglei, and Malet filed a criminal self-complaint against the Chinese persons in charge, accusing them of fraud and breach of trust. The Chinese depositors of the bank also followed suit and filed lawsuits against Gu Yubo and others. After investigations by the First Special District Court, Gu Yubo, Liu Tongfu, and Shen Jingzhong were either wanted or the trial was suspended due to their whereabouts being unknown. Bao Ziwen and Chen Yizai, who were in custody, were each ordered to

Post 8,000 Yuan Bail

And Sun Wenkui was entrusted to his lawyer Lin Shenqing for bail. Lin Kanghou, Zhang Xusheng, Li Yichou, Qian Chengxu, Wu Chunlei, Wang Zhonglin, and others were ordered to appear for questioning. All of these details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng opened the court for a continuation of the trial. The defendants Bao, Chen, and Sun, as well as Wu Chunlei, all appeared in court in person. Zhang, Li, Wang, Qian, and Lin Kanghou were still represented by their defense lawyers. The lawyers for the British directors Yelu and others submitted the Meihua Bank's

Shareholder List

Stating that Bao and Chen were both shareholders of the bank. The list was shown to Bao and Chen in court, but they both denied it, claiming that they had never seen the list and that it was fabricated. The court then summoned the two British directors, Menglei and Yelu, and Malet, to testify one by one about the relationship between the defendants Bao and Chen and Meihua Bank. All three stated that when they dined with Gu Yubo and Li Yichou, Gu and Li said that Bao was a major Chinese shareholder and was elected as a director by the Chinese shareholders, and that Chen was a shareholder and also served as deputy manager. In fact,

There Were Only Two Chinese Directors

Gu and Li. According to British law, the quota for Chinese directors was set at two. Later, although a third seat was added for the Chinese and Bao assumed the position, it was never realized, and the bank collapsed. Therefore, Bao's qualifications as a director were never recognized by the British Consulate. Upon questioning, Bao and Chen both denied being shareholders of Meihua Bank and holding positions as directors or deputy managers. As for the photo of all the directors taken on the bank's opening day, in which Bao was included, Bao claimed that because he

Went to the Bank to Congratulate

And was talking to Li Yichou when the photo was taken, he was included in the photo. Later, the court re-examined the receipt submitted by lawyer Lin Luanqing in the past, which showed that Bao and Chen had received salaries for March. The plaintiff's agent lawyer, Wu Peng, submitted a list of Meihua employees, and the bailiffs requested by Yelu and others submitted books showing that Bao, Chen, and Sun all had deposits. Each item was shown to them, but Bao and Chen

Absolutely Denied

Holding any position, receiving any salary, and denied having any deposits in Meihua. Sun Wenkui also said that he had no deposits. Therefore, Jiang Yiping, the defense lawyer for Bao and Chen, requested that an accountant be selected to thoroughly audit the entire accounts of the bank, saying that otherwise, the inside story of this entire scam would be difficult to expose. The audit fee should be borne by Bao and Chen, who were extremely willing to do so. Judge Huang stated that the case should be investigated further and adjourned the trial for further investigation.

Huang Weiru and Zhu Ziyun Counter-Accuse Each Other; Court Judgment; The Zhu Brothers' Medical Practice Is Believable; Huang's Lawsuit Arises from Misunderstanding and Is Not False Accusation

Huang Weiru, a local resident, recently suffered from a throat ailment and went to the clinic of throat specialist Zhu Ziyun to get a number for treatment. Unexpectedly, the person providing the consultation at that time was not Zhu himself. Huang believed that he had come to the clinic because of his reputation, but Zhu was using someone else to practice medicine under his name, which was deceitful. Therefore, afterwards, he accused Zhu of fraud and breach of trust at the First Special District Local Court, requesting that Zhu Ziyun be summoned and punished according to Articles 339 and 342 of the Criminal Law. After being accused, Zhu hired lawyer Lu Qi to defend himself and filed a counterclaim against Huang. Judge Chuan Lin had already

summoned both parties

for interrogation and declared Zhu and Huang not guilty. This was previously reported in this newspaper. Now, the judgment of this case has been delivered to both parties yesterday. The reasons for the judgment are described in two parts, self-accusation and counterclaim. The self-accusation part states that the facts of a crime should be determined by evidence. The plaintiff in this case claims that the defendant, Zhu Ziyun, practices medicine in Xian Hu Alley, Zhoujiazui Road. On October 8 of this year, the plaintiff, suffering from a throat illness, knew that the defendant was a throat specialist. On that day, in the early morning, he specially went to register and paid

a special registration

fee of two yuan and forty cents for treatment. However, the doctor was not the defendant himself. It was Luo who used his name as a slogan and replaced him with a person with no experience to diagnose, in order to defraud patients of money, which is fraud and breach of trust. He requested that the defendant be punished according to the law and presented two pieces of film hanging with the sign of Zhu Ziyun's medical residence as evidence in court. During the interrogation of the defendant, he claimed that his medical residence was jointly run by him and his brother Zhu Zhongyun, and Zhu Zhongyun was also a doctor with

a National Medical Association

membership certificate and a health bureau license as proof. He also submitted many old prescriptions returned by patients. After reviewing the prescriptions, there were the words "Zhu Brothers' Clinic Stationery". It is credible that the defendant claimed that the brothers practiced medicine together. The film submitted by the plaintiff, the sign of Zhu Ziyun's medical residence, was attached to the side of the China-Upper Pond Pharmacy signboard, not the sign hanging at the defendant's door. It cannot be simply assumed that the defendant has a false name calling for

defrauding patients

of money based on this film alone. Moreover, the evidence presented by the defendant confirms that he and his brother practice medicine together. Even if the defendant himself did not come out for treatment on the day the plaintiff sought medical treatment, he cannot be said to have violated good faith. The counterclaim part states that the crime of false accusation requires the intention to subject another person to criminal or disciplinary punishment by fabricating facts as its constituent element. The counterclaimant in this case did not personally

receive medical treatment from the brothers

of the defendant in the counterclaim, as admitted by the defendant in the counterclaim himself. Although the counterclaimant is

practicing medicine with his brothers

, the counterclaimant suspected that the medical residence was solely established by the defendant in the counterclaim because there was a sign of Zhu Ziyun's medical residence next to the signboard of the China-Upper Pond Pharmacy. Because he believed in the medical skills of the counterclaimant, he registered for treatment but did not see the person he wanted to see in his heart, accusing him of calling for an empty name and defrauding patients of money. This kind of behavior clearly arises from misunderstanding. It is difficult to simply regard it as having constituted the elements of the crime of false accusation. In summary, based on Articles 293, Paragraph 1, 332, and 335 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the judgment is made according to the main text.

Unable to Afford a Wedding, A Car is Used for a Kidnapping Wedding

Jiang Qinghua, a native of Gaoyou, 23 years old, who lives in a bungalow without a number in Yangshupu, works as a worker in the Dongyang Cotton Mill on the same road. Six years ago, he was engaged to Han Jinlin (19 years old), a girl from the same village. Her father, Han Ronggen, works in the Tongxing Cotton Mill and lives at No. 10 Yuezhou Road. Jiang Qinghua's mother died of illness a month ago. Later, he asked a matchmaker to ask the girl's father to choose an auspicious day for the wedding, because Han Ronggen wanted a betrothal gift of 240 yuan and 17 pieces of clothing before he would agree to the marriage. Unable to resolve the matter, at 7:30 PM on the 19th, he hired a car with his elder brother Jiang Yanyuan and cousin Zhu Jiangshi and drove to Han's house. While the girl's father, Ronggen, and elder brother, Baofu, were still working at the Tongchang Cotton Mill and had not returned home, they dragged the girl out of the bedroom, pulled her into the car (commonly known as a kidnapping wedding), and drove her back to his home, forcing her to worship heaven and earth. Later, Zhu Jiangshi took off the girl's pants and hid them on the bed, preventing her from taking a single step beyond the bed. Waiting for the girl's father to react aggressively, the girl could not escape and cried bitterly on the bed. Han Ronggen and his son returned home from the factory and learned the whole story from the second landlord, Xin Linfa, a native of Ningbo. They reported to the Huishan Police Station. Detectives Sun Aizhong and Shen Binkui secretly went to the address and arrested Jiang Qinghua, Jiang Qiyuan, and Zhu Jiangshi. They put the girl in her lower clothes and took them all to the police station. The girl was taken back by her father, and Jiang Qinghua, his brother, and Zhu were detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special District Court and questioned by Judge Xiao Xiefen at the Third Criminal Court. The girl said that she had to be welcomed with a sedan chair, and her father, Han Ronggen, also demanded a supplementary betrothal gift of 200 yuan and to be carried in a sedan chair. After Judge Xiao advised both parties, he sentenced Jiang Qinghua, Jiang Qiyuan, and Zhu Jiangshi to one month of imprisonment each, suspended for two years.

anecdotes are numerous

So, Mr. Hill entered the museum and secretly took a huge famous painting and left, hiding it for twelve hours. For a time, the police and law enforcement agencies were panicked. residing in Inner Mongolia

for over a year, and later making shorter stays in Beijing, Shanghai, and Nanjing. At that time, Nanjing had just become the new capital, and everything was still simple. watched the war for five months

While in China, he will visit Chairman Chiang and other officials. Mr. Lies,

initially in Paris

served as a reporter for the Politiken newspaper for two years, then as a news editor, and then as a special correspondent for the newspaper in Europe, South America, North Africa, Greenland, and Iceland. During the Sino-Russian War, he accompanied the King of Abyssinia to Taixi and almost met with disaster. This time, he came to China from Denmark with his wife, passing through Abyssinia, Manchuria, Jehol, and Zhangjiakou. After that, he came to Shanghai from North China. When he goes to the mainland next week, his wife plans to stay in Shanghai. The couple is scheduled to return to their country in February of next year. Mr. Hill plans to linger in Shanghai for a while before entering the mainland again.

Minhang Ferry Overturns; More Male and Female Bodies Retrieved; Total of Fourteen; Public Organizations Discuss Aftermath

At around 11:00 AM on the 22nd of this month, the Luo A'gou ferry in Minhang Town, South Shanghai, overturned in Peimian due to wind. In addition to the 16 men and women rescued on the spot, including He Qingtian, Li Yousheng, Yuan A'fa from Zhugang Township, He Chunquan, Ding Yousheng from Dingqiao Township, and the boat owner Luo A'gou Jiang Chunquan, there were more than 20 other passengers who were not rescued and drowned tragically. Later, Zhang Jingqing, the district chief of the First District of the town's water public security, and Wang Xingyuan, the captain of the special task force, supervised the patrol boats and hired more than ten temporary net boats to work with the water police to retrieve the bodies of Li Yishou, Zhu Yunpu, Wang Ziqing, Pan A'bao, Li Jinru, He A'tu, He Xiangeng, Wang Guansheng, Wang Wangshi, and other nine men and women from the Huangpu River. The family members took them back with a written guarantee for burial. The details were reported in the previous newspaper. Later, because the tide of the Peijiang River rose sharply for a while, it was not easy to salvage. Until the day before yesterday, the drowned bodies floated to the surface of the river. Fourteen more men and women were recovered, including Zhao Yousheng, 59 years old, residing in Chen Chunxiang's household, 1st Bao 1st Jia 7th household, Ruan Jincai, 32 years old, residing in 1st Bao 5th Jia 1st household, Li Jingen, 25 years old, residing in 1st Bao 6th Jia 7th household, Li Guoqing, 5 years old (Li Jingen's son), Li Zhushi, 31 years old, residing in 1st Bao 6th Jia 8th household, Zhang Jinsong, 45 years old, residing in 1st Bao 8th Jia 9th household, Lu Botian, Zhu Jihai, ages unknown, residing in 2nd Bao, He Kunsheng, 27 years old, residing in 3rd Bao 4th Jia 1st household. The above ten bodies were all from Zhugang Township. Ma Jinsheng, 18 years old, residing in 5th Bao, Fei Sihai, 34 years old, residing in 4th Bao. The above two bodies were from Dingqiao Township. Wang Jialu, 31 years old, residing in Xiaotang, Liu Qianshi, 24 years old, residing in Wujiaqiao. The above two bodies were from Dongtai. All of them have been claimed by their families for burial. Only Li Jingen and Li Guoqing, father and son, drowned. After the incident, his mother, Li Yangshi (53 years old), cried and fainted at home and died of grief soon after. A family of three generations, grandfather, father and son, died unnaturally. It is now reported that local public organizations are gathering to discuss the aftermath and to provide compensation to the families of the deceased. The boat owners Luo A'gou and Jiang Chunquan have been requested by the families of the deceased to be handed over to the Fengxian County court for legal action.

Taxpayer Association Letter to the Municipal Council to Stop Water Cuts

Why Not Notify of Increased Deposits? Company Responsible for Dangers

The Chinese Taxpayer Association of the Public Concession yesterday sent a letter to the Municipal Council, stating, "Dear Sirs, we have recently received a letter from the Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association of Yangzhou, which states, 'We have learned from our Standing Committee member, Mr. Li Zhixi, that I have a house at No. 11, Lane 62, Jishan Lane, Songpan Road, East District, Yangshupu, six shops at the entrance of Lane 55, opposite this lane, No. 47, and a house at No. 16, Xiuren Fang, Zhoujiapai Road, totaling more than forty rooms, with more than three hundred tenants inside. For decades, we have used the Shanghai Waterworks Company's water and have never owed fees. On the morning of the 26th of this month, the company suddenly cut off the drinking water to the above three places. Initially, we thought it was because the water bill for this month had not been paid, and we immediately sent the fee and asked them to quickly reconnect the line. However, the company replied that this cut was not for overdue fees. If we want to continue using water, we need to add a deposit of 160 yuan for all three places. I then investigated the neighboring Kuoyu Lane, Jingsui Lane, Songmao Fang, and Mingde Lane. The deposits for each household are still the same. I don't know why they are increasing only for my place. Moreover, the company did not send a single piece of paper to inform us beforehand and immediately took such resolute measures, which seems to be disallowed even by legal persons. Moreover, water and fire are essential for people and cannot be without them for a day. Cutting off people's drinking water is tantamount to cutting off people's lives. Now, more than three hundred tenants are pressing us and there is no end to the blaming. I have no choice but to hire workers to carry water for supply, temporarily avoiding a disturbance. However, the matter concerns the safety of more than three hundred people, and we are forced to ask the association to convey this to the Chinese Taxpayer Association and ask it to strictly prohibit the company and order it to restore the water to its original state immediately. If the company delays again and dangers or other accidents occur as a result, and all losses this time, the company must be fully responsible. As for increasing the deposit, we will follow the public's decision and not hold dissenting opinions, etc.' The association believes that increasing the deposit is a whole plan of the company and should not be directed at individuals, and it is another issue. Since there was no prior notification, how can it be justified to cut off people's drinking water? Such oppressive behavior is truly beyond the norm of the commercial market. Your association is the guarantor for Chinese taxpayers, so we specially and solemnly ask you to uphold justice and strictly order the company to release the water immediately to avoid accidents, etc. We hope so." The association believes that the waterworks company did not notify in advance about increasing the deposit and then immediately used resolute measures to cut off people's drinking water, causing the lives of more than three hundred citizens to be hindered. This method is not only inconsistent with commercial norms but also sufficient to affect social order. In addition to reserving all claims for compensation for losses caused by the water cut, we are specially writing to request your bureau to quickly and strictly order the waterworks company to immediately release the water to avoid serious accidents. We hope so. To the General Office of the Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council, Shanghai Municipal

Resolution of the Osram Trademark Dispute The German firm Osram Trading Company in this city originally used the "Osram Trading Company" as the trademark for Osram light bulbs. Later, the Huiming Factory used the four characters "Osram Brand" on the batteries produced by the factory. The Osram Trading Company, considering that it had not given its consent and the unauthorized use of the same name would easily cause confusion to the outside world, requested the Trademark Bureau to prohibit other companies from using the "Osram" trademark. The trademark of the Huiming Factory was cancelled, but the factory refused to accept this, arguing that the Osram Trading Company had not registered the trademark and petitioned the Trademark Bureau to review the case. The Osram Trading Company argued that since its company name had not been permitted, no one should be allowed to use it, and registration was irrelevant. The Trademark Bureau handled the matter impartially and ordered the Huiming Factory not to use the "Osram" name anymore.

School and Social Education Institutions Teachers and Staff Should Pay Income Tax Elementary School Teachers and Staff Are Exempted The Jiangsu Education Department Specifically Notifies All Schools to Comply

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, regarding whether the income tax of school teachers and staff should be collected at the same time as civil servants, and whether staff of county-level social education institutions can be exempted, has not been clearly stipulated. Therefore, it has specially requested instructions from the provincial government. The provincial government, according to the report, stated that teachers and staff of provincial and county-level schools (except for elementary school teachers and staff, who are exempted), and staff of social education institutions, are all within the scope of civil servants, and those whose salaries reach 3,000 yuan per month should have their income tax collected at the same time as civil servants. The department was specifically instructed to relay this to all schools and social education institutions for compliance.

General Overview of National Education (3)

— Lei Zhen

(Lecture at the Vocational Guidance Class of Specialized Schools)

Universities and independent colleges aim to study advanced knowledge and cultivate specialized talents. They recruit high school graduates and have a longer duration of study than specialized schools. Medical schools have five years, and other colleges have four years. Universities are divided into colleges of liberal arts, science, law, education, engineering, business, medicine, and agriculture. A school must have three or more colleges, and one of the colleges must be in science, agriculture, engineering, or medicine, to be called a university. If there is only one or two colleges, it cannot be called a university, but only a "College of..." For example, the National Shanghai College of Commerce has only one college of commerce, so it is called the Shanghai College of Commerce. Another example is the private Ginling Women's Arts and Science College, which consists of the College of Liberal Arts and the College of Science, but does not have three colleges, so it is called Ginling Women's Arts and Science College, and cannot be called Ginling Women's University. According to the Ministry of Education's statistics for the 21st and 22nd academic years, there are a total of 41 universities nationwide, including 13 national universities, 8 provincial universities, and 20 private universities. There are a total of 38 independent colleges nationwide, including national colleges, 11 provincial colleges, and 22 private colleges. There are a total of 79 universities and independent colleges. Among these 79 schools, 48 have colleges of liberal arts, 31 have colleges of law, 16 have colleges of commerce, and 13 have colleges of education. These belong to the liberal arts category, totaling 108 colleges. 41 have colleges of science, 22 have colleges of engineering, 13 have colleges of medicine, and 13 have colleges of agriculture. These belong to the science and engineering category, totaling 89 colleges. In terms of national universities and independent colleges, there are more colleges in the liberal arts category. There are a total of 37,257 students in national universities and independent colleges, including 19,139 in public institutions and 18,118 in private institutions. Comparing public and private institutions, the number of students is not very different, but the number of schools is greater in private institutions (37 public institutions and 42 private institutions), which is the opposite of specialized schools. Furthermore, the total number of students in specialized schools, universities, and independent colleges is 41,768. Separating by field of study, there are 15,698 science and engineering students in the colleges of science, agriculture, engineering, and medicine, and 26,041 liberal arts students in the colleges of liberal arts, law, commerce, and education. (28 students have not been assigned to a college and are not included in the percentage calculation). The percentage is 63.39% for liberal arts and 37.61% for science and engineering. There are almost twice as many liberal arts students as science and engineering students.

The distribution of national universities, independent colleges, and specialized schools also varies greatly. The place with the most is Shanghai, with 27 schools. The place with the least is one school, such as in Anhui and Yunnan provinces. Some provinces do not have a single school, such as Guizhou province. This is due to transportation and cultural factors. In the future, we should pay attention to adding one or two schools in places without schools above the specialized level to adjust higher education.

University graduate schools recruit university undergraduates to study advanced academics and provide a place for faculty to research. The research period is at least two years. They are located within universities or independent colleges and are divided into graduate schools of liberal arts, science, law, education, agriculture, commerce, and medicine. Those with three or more graduate schools are called graduate schools, and those that have not established three graduate schools are only called a certain graduate school, not a graduate school. There are ten universities and one college in China with graduate schools, namely the National Central University's Graduate School of Science, Department of Mathematics, Graduate School of Agriculture, Department of Agronomy, Peking University's Graduate School of Liberal Arts, Department of Chinese Literature and History, Graduate School of Science, Department of Mathematics, Department of Physics, Department of Chemistry, Graduate School of Law, Tsinghua University's Graduate School of Liberal Arts, Department of Chinese Literature, Department of Foreign Languages, Department of Philosophy, Department of History, Graduate School of Science, Department of Physics, Department of Chemistry, Department of Mathematics, Department of Biology, Graduate School of Law, Department of Political Science, Department of Economics, Wuhan University's Graduate School of Engineering, Department of Civil Engineering, Graduate School of Law, Department of Economics, Sun Yat-sen University's Graduate School of Liberal Arts, Department of Chinese Language and Literature, Department of History, Graduate School of Education, Department of Education, Department of
