It is difficult to generalize, but most cases are due to ovarian dysfunction. (2) With proper treatment, there should be no major problems. (3) See (1) and (2). Abdominal distension after intercourse is common and not a cause for concern. Urinary incontinence is also caused by mental excitement. (4) Oral or injectable "female hormone preparations," such as (Ovarin Substancc) (Because you are a fellow professional, I will not elaborate on the details as I would for a regular patient.) (5) In addition to the above medicine, also take "Tancno," three times a day, one teaspoon each time, until menstruation returns. (6) Yes, but bird's nest and white fungus do not have much nutritional value. (7) "Livemin" and Easton's Syrup. (8) Regulate bowel movements, promote nutrition, engage in appropriate exercise (not too strenuous), reduce sexual activity (once a week or every half month). (9) Gynecologists can all treat this.

Random Talk

The Hezhong Company Case Occurs Again in Baoyuan

— Rong

According to a Tianjin dispatch, the Hezhong Company case has occurred again in Baoyuan. The case involves two unlicensed Japanese residents, Tanaka Yoshio and Takeda Yoneo, who arrived in Baoyuan on the 8th and bribed a traitorous citizen to rent a house in their name, establishing the Hezhong Company for smuggling and drug trafficking. The landlord, aware of the true situation, feared being punished and reported it to the authorities. The Jin Court sentenced the tenant to imprisonment and ordered Tanaka to vacate the house, but he refused. The court, according to common practice in Chinese lawsuits, sealed the house. Tanaka tore off the seals and complained to the Kono Special Service Agency, protesting. Unlicensed foreign residents arbitrarily bribing traitors in the interior to organize smuggling and drug trafficking agencies has already violated international practice. The court, acting according to common Chinese lawsuit practice, sealed the house, but Tanaka tore off the seals, showing extreme contempt for our national authorities.

Not only is the other party unaware of their wrongdoing, but they have also lodged a serious protest, using the pretext of protecting foreign residents to increase military police deployment. The Japanese military has even stated that if negotiations are unsuccessful, they will take self-defense actions. Is this the explanation of self-defense actions? It is truly a different interpretation, truly unheard of. Ambassador Kawagoe is currently stationed in Beijing, intending to adjust Sino-Japanese relations with our national authorities, but on one hand, they are creating smuggling and drug trafficking incidents in Baoyuan, and on the other hand, they are conducting large-scale military exercises in Pingjin. Therefore, the Washington Post stated that this Japanese maneuver is a military action with a clear purpose, evidently intended to force the Chinese government to accept its demands regarding North China. This maneuver is nothing more than a demonstration of force. The American media's observation is naturally very clear, and can our nation, both government and people, view this action as justified and remain indifferent?

However, international negotiations have their normal course. Assuming there is genuine intention to negotiate through diplomatic channels, there should be no more extraordinary actions in North China. Assuming they wish to take free action by force, they are free to do so, but why must they take the form of negotiations again? On one hand, the envoy is negotiating with our government authorities in Beijing, while on the other hand, they disregard everything and take free action. The complete lack of sincerity in these negotiations is evident. Furthermore, according to yesterday's Tokyo dispatch, the content of the new instructions for Sino-Japanese negotiations brought by Consul General Suma stated that the fundamental spirit of these instructions is that Japan's demands have not changed and that there is no way to deviate from the initially determined goals. If this is the case, then the Japanese side is completely unwilling to compromise, and our country can only devise strategies for self-preservation and self-rescue. Is there any other way out?

According to a London dispatch, due to the Spanish Civil War and the increasing power of fascist groups in Europe, Soviet Russia's international position has been greatly weakened. Today, it is preparing a self-defense plan to resist without external assistance. This statement is true. A country cannot rely on others for assistance if it cannot save itself. Our entire population, under this worst of circumstances, should think of self-reliance, self-rescue, and be prepared to make the ultimate sacrifice for the country. Do not rely on others, and do not fear others. We should respond calmly to overcome this harsh environment and be worthy of being citizens of the Republic of China. Rong

Real Estate Assessment Association

— Rong

(Inland Correspondence) "Real Estate Assessment Association" is a name coined by the author, because although there are many "public servants" wearing badges on their lapels in the streets and alleys asking house and property owners to fill out a form and appraise the prices of houses and properties, this "public service" agency has not been formally established. Since there is no formal agency, naturally there is no need to pre-announce the name. For the sake of convenience, the author will tentatively call it a "Real Estate Assessment Association." I think that in the future, it will only change a few words. It has been decided that real estate will be evaluated and there is no way to change that.
